  - numeric inspection helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\the` now narrow-materializes count-register and scratch-counter values as conservative digit tokens just like `\number`, and it now also narrow-materializes dimen-register / skip-register / `\newlength` payload as conservative `pt` text, while dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin both direct output and `\edef` capture paths under later option-only revisions
  - protected expanded-definition aliases are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\protected@edef` and `\protected@xdef` now reuse the same narrow `\edef` / `\xdef` expansion and grouped-global persistence paths under `\makeatletter`, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both local capture and grouped global capture under a later option-only revision
  - LaTeX counter-format helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` preamble-definition level: `\@arabic`, `\@roman`, `\@Roman`, `\@alph`, and `\@Alph` now narrow-materialize count-like macro arguments as common counter text, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both direct output and `\edef` capture paths under a later option-only revision
  - builtin zero-arg text/meta helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\space`, `\@backslashchar`, `\@percentchar`, and `\@hashchar` now expand as visible macro payload instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both direct output and `\edef` capture paths under a later option-only revision
  - command declaration prefixes are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\global` now narrow-promotes grouped `\def`, `\let`, `\newif`, `\newcount`, `\countdef`, `\newcommand`, `\renewcommand`, `\providecommand`, `\DeclareRobustCommand`, and `\@namedef` paths into the outer scope instead of letting them evaporate at group end, while `\long`, `\protected`, and `\outer` now behave as non-visible declaration prefixes instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - next-token lookahead is now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\futurelet` now narrow-binds the looked-ahead token without consuming it, `\global\futurelet` can promote that binding across grouped preamble setup, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins the common lookahead path under a later option-only revision
  - token-stringification is now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\string` now prints the next control-sequence name or character token without expanding it, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both control-sequence and character-token paths under a later option-only revision
  - roman numeral expansion is now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition level: `\romannumeral` now prints lowercase Roman numerals for positive integer expressions and suppresses nonpositive values, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level scratch-counter helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\advance` now narrow-updates count registers, the common scratch aliases `\count@`, `\@tempcnta`, and `\@tempcntb` now narrow-map onto stable VM count registers, the numeric constant macros `\z@`, `\@ne`, `\tw@`, `\thr@@`, and `\m@ne` now participate in `\ifnum`, `\number`, count assignment, and `\advance`, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level scratch dimen/glue arithmetic is now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\advance` now narrow-updates dimen and skip registers instead of only count registers, `\multiply` / `\divide` now narrow-reuse that same arithmetic path for dimen and skip registers instead of staying count-only, `\newdimen` / `\newskip` aliases and builtin scratch dimen/skip helpers keep participating in the same `\the` / `pt` readback path, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin both additive and multiplicative dimen/glue arithmetic under later option-only revisions
  - low-level numeric/character/token-kind branch guards are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\if` now narrow-expands simple control-sequence aliases down to character tokens before comparing them, `\ifodd` now narrow-checks number expressions and scratch counters instead of falling through as an undefined conditional, `\ifdim` now narrow-compares dimen/skip expressions instead of falling through as an undefined conditional, `\ifcat` now narrow-compares control-sequence kinds and character catcodes instead of falling through as an undefined conditional, `\ifcase...\or...\else...\fi` now narrow-selects numbered branches (including else fallback) without leaking skipped branches into output, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin character, odd/even, dimen/glue, token-kind, and case-branch paths under later option-only revisions
  - low-level conditional prefixes are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\unless` now narrow-inverts the next common conditional helper instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, its one-shot negate flag survives snapshot/restore, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both scratch-counter and `\ifcsname...\endcsname` paths under a later option-only revision
  - low-level group-exit helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\aftergroup` now narrow-reinjects pending tokens when the current group closes instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, pending token queues survive snapshot/restore, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins grouped assignment-hook paths under a later option-only revision
  - low-level assignment-complete helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\afterassignment` now narrow-reinjects a one-shot token when the next supported assignment primitive (`\def`, `\let`, `\count`, `\advance`, `\multiply`, `\divide`, `\newcount`, `\countdef`) succeeds instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, its pending token survives snapshot/restore, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins count-assignment hook paths under a later option-only revision
  - low-level scratch-counter arithmetic helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\multiply` and `\divide` now narrow-update count registers and the same scratch aliases `\count@`, `\@tempcnta`, and `\@tempcntb` instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, integer arithmetic through `\number`/`\ifnum` survives snapshot restore, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level character-definition helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\chardef` now narrow-defines visible character tokens that also participate in number expressions, TeX-style backtick char constants are now narrow-read in the same integer scanner, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both direct output and `\number`/`\edef` capture paths under a later option-only revision
  - low-level stringification helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: plain `\escapechar` now narrow-acts like a count alias with the default prefix value `92`, `\string` now narrow-honors that prefix both at runtime and inside `\edef`, `\detokenize` and `\meaning` reuse the same control-sequence prefix instead of hard-coding `\`, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins prefix changes under a later option-only revision
  - low-level line-ending helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: plain `\endlinechar` now narrow-acts like a count alias for plain `\read ... to ...` and `\readline ... to ...`, values in `0..=255` now append a visible line-ending character before tokenization instead of silently dropping it, negative values keep the existing no-suffix path, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins revision-driven suffix changes under a later option-only revision
  - low-level definition-scope helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: plain `\globaldefs` now narrow-acts like a count alias, positive values now force grouped `\def`/`\let`/`\newif`/`\newcommand` definitions global without an explicit `\global` prefix, negative values now narrow-suppress even explicit `\global` definitions back to local scope, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins grouped option-driven definition persistence under a later option-only revision
  - low-level count-register definition helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\newcount` now narrow-allocates stable count-register aliases, `\countdef` now narrow-binds a control sequence to an explicit count register number instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, allocator progress survives snapshot restore, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both paths under a later option-only revision
  - low-level counter-command helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\setcounter`, `\addtocounter`, `\stepcounter`, and `\refstepcounter` now narrow-update `\newcount\c@...`-style LaTeX counters instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, `\value{...}` now narrow-materializes those counters as digit tokens in both execution and `\edef` capture paths, public `\arabic/\roman/\Roman/\alph/\Alph` now narrow-read the same `c@...` counters in addition to low-level `\@arabic/\@roman/\@Roman/\@alph/\@Alph`, `\makeatletter`-scoped `\@addtoreset` now narrow-records child-counter reset relations, `\@removefromreset` now narrow-removes them again, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin both reset and unreset paths under later option-only revisions
  - low-level dimen/length/glue helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\newdimen`, `\dimendef`, plain `\dimen`, `\newskip`, `\skipdef`, plain `\skip`, public `\newlength`, `\setlength`, and `\addtolength` now narrow-allocate/register/update snapshot-aware dimen-or-glue state instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, builtin scratch dimen aliases (`\dimen@`, `\@tempdima`, `\@tempdimb`), builtin scratch skip aliases (`\skip@`, `\@tempskipa`, `\@tempskipb`), plus `\p@` are now available for common package internals, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin both direct `\the` rendering and `\edef` capture paths under later option-only revisions
  - low-level token-register helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\newtoks` now narrow-allocates stable token-register aliases, `\toksdef` now narrow-binds a control sequence to an explicit token register number, plain `\toks` assignment now stores grouped token-list payloads in snapshot-aware VM state instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, `\the` now narrow-materializes those stored token lists alongside count-register inspection, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins alias-definition, direct assignment, and `\edef` capture paths under a later option-only revision
  - control-sequence existence guards are now also fixed and covered at the same local preamble path: `\ifcsname...\endcsname` now narrow-checks whether the constructed control-sequence name is already defined instead of falling through as an undefined conditional, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both present and absent branches under a later option-only revision
  - `minted` v3 cache is now fixed and covered at the narrow cache-input level: `\IfFileExists` can detect local `_minted-*/*.pygtex` cache files and feed them back through `\input` in both VM and internal compiler smoke paths
  - optional config/asset loading is now also fixed and covered at the narrow input-helper level: `\InputIfFileExists` can input local `*.cfg` files while still choosing success/fallback branches, `\ProvidesFile` now records provided dates for those loaded config files in VM snapshot state, and dedicated corpus fixtures now exercise that path from both wrapper packages and wrapper classes through deletion/recovery and later option-only revisions
  - corpus realism has now moved one step past isolated micro-fixtures: a dedicated split-preamble bibliography-workflow fixture combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, multi-`.bbl` bibliography ingestion, and concrete `semantic.aux` `\bibstyle{...}` / `\bibdata{...}` / `\bibcite{...}` artifact drift, while later revisions pin an option-only change, a bibliography-order change, a semantically equal `.bbl` edit, a semantic-change `.bbl` edit, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, nested preamble failure/recovery, local package/class failure/recovery, and body include failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a larger mixed-paper fixture: `split-preamble-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, short-title TOC, LOF writes, figure caption/reference rewrite, appendix/theorem/`nameref` rewrite, natbib author-year citations, bibliography drift, option-only change, semantically equal `.bbl` edit, semantic-change `.bbl` edit, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a larger biblatex mixed-paper fixture: `split-preamble-biblatex-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, short-title TOC, LOF writes, figure caption/reference rewrite, appendix/theorem/`nameref` rewrite, `\textcite` / `\parencite` / `\printbibliography`, bibliography-order drift, semantically equal `.bbl` edit, semantic-change `.bbl` edit, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a manual-TOC larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-manual-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, `\phantomsection` / `\addcontentsline`, short-title TOC, LOF writes, figure caption/reference rewrite, appendix/theorem/`nameref` rewrite, natbib author-year citations, bibliography drift, option-only change, semantically equal `.bbl` edit, semantic-change `.bbl` edit, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a manual-TOC biblatex larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-manual-biblatex-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, `\phantomsection` / `\addcontentsline`, short-title TOC, LOF writes, figure caption/reference rewrite, appendix/theorem/`nameref` rewrite, `\textcite` / `\parencite` / `\printbibliography`, bibliography-order drift, semantically equal `.bbl` edit, semantic-change `.bbl` edit, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a reference-heavy larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-reference-mixed-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` preamble inputs, equation/float/label/range/title refs plus cleveref/capitalized variants, option-only change, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a manual-heading/bibliography/caption larger workflow: `split-preamble-manual-bibliography-caption-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, manual TOC, bibliography heading, figure caption/list, theorem/appendix/reference semantics, bibliography drift, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a theorem-heavy larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-heading-theorem-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` preamble inputs, manual TOC, bibliography heading, theorem/shared-counter drift, appendix, figure/captionof/list semantics, semantically equal `.bbl`, semantic-change `.bbl`, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a package-wrapper-heavy larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-package-wrapper-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` preamble inputs, `hyperref + cleveref + varioref + theorem/appendix/float/reference` interaction, short-title/manual TOC, equation/float/label/range/title refs, option-only drift, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a bibliography tool-version larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-bibliography-toolversion-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, a wrapper-heavy `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/toolchain}` preamble inputs, bibliography style/input/tool-version drift, semantically equal `.bbl`, semantic-change `.bbl`, partial `.bbl` loss/recovery, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a package-interaction larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-package-interaction-paper-family-workflow` combines the same wrapper-heavy project shape with `hyperref + cleveref + varioref + theorem/appendix/float/reference` interaction, bibliography drift, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes a longer failure/semantic chain larger paper-family fixture: `split-preamble-failure-semantic-chain-paper-family-workflow` combines wrapper option forwarding, bibliography drift, semantic-change rebuilds, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure/recovery into one longer revision chain with structured `FAIL-JSON-EXPECT.txt`
  - those larger paper-family recovery revisions (`REV10/12/14/16`) now also pin `rebuilt_page_count`, `reused_page_count`, and `semantic_pass_count` in `build-meta.json`, so recovery behavior is no longer checked only via `semantic_aux_backdated`
  - representative larger bibliography/paper-family fixture now also pin `semantic-index.json` as structured JSON instead of only substring artifacts: `split-preamble-bibliography-workflow` / `split-preamble-paper-family-workflow` lock base shape plus bibliography input-order/style drift, while `split-preamble-biblatex-paper-family-workflow` / `split-preamble-manual-biblatex-paper-family-workflow` lock base shape plus bibliography input-order and heading/manual-title drift
  - replay invalidation is now tighter for semantic-changing bibliography inputs too: when a changed `.bbl` is part of the current bibliography set and semantic aux actually drifts, the final semantic build reruns from the base snapshot instead of reusing the preamble checkpoint, which prevents stale preamble bibliography prefixes from surviving into later revisions while still allowing semantically-equal `.bbl` edits to keep page reuse
  - renderer/session hardening also now includes a narrow Phase 4/5 prewarm-observability path: viewport prewarm no longer eagerly fills full-page raster PNG cache, but instead prioritizes current page -> visible pages -> adjacent pages, suppresses same revision/page/zoom inflight duplicate work, and sends actor-owned warm requests that exercise renderer-native tile/session state while recording dedicated prewarm/skip/fallback-prewarm metrics, recent events, and aggregate latency summaries
  - corpus realism also now includes `split-preamble-biblatex-citation-workflow`, which combines wrapper option forwarding, nested preamble `\input`, `\textcite`, `\parencite`, `\printbibliography`, bibliography drift, option-only change, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure-recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes `split-preamble-biblatex-multicite-workflow`, which combines wrapper option forwarding, nested preamble `\input`, `\textcites`, `\parencites`, `\printbibliography`, option-only change, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure-recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes `split-preamble-bibliography-metadata-workflow`, which combines wrapper option forwarding, nested preamble `\input`, `\citeauthor`, `\citeyear`, `\citetitle`, `\citefield{doi,eprint}`, bibliography drift, partial `.bbl` loss, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure-recovery in the same project
  - corpus realism also now includes `split-preamble-bibliography-date-workflow`, which combines wrapper option forwarding, nested preamble `\input`, `\citedate`, `\Citedate`, `\citeurldate`, `\Citeurldate`, bibliography drift, partial `.bbl` loss, and nested preamble/package/class/body failure-recovery in the same project

  - low-level package-internal sanitizing hooks are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@onelevel@sanitize` now behaves as a non-visible narrow no-op helper instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision

  - low-level package-internal branch helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@firstoftwo`, `\@secondoftwo`, `\@gobble`, `\@gobbletwo`, `\@gobblethree`, and `\@gobblefour` now narrow-select or discard arguments instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, and dedicated corpus fixtures pin those paths under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision

  - low-level expansion aliases are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@xp` and `\@xa` now narrow-delegate to `\expandafter` instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, makeatletter alias `\@nx` now narrow-delegates to the same full-expansion `\noexpand` path inside `\edef`/`\xdef`, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins those paths under a wrapper class/package stack with later option-only revisions

  - low-level package-internal optional-default helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@testopt` now narrow-injects a default optional argument when no `[...]` form is present, `\@dblarg` now narrow-rewrites a missing optional argument into the doubled `[arg]{arg}` form common in wrapper macros, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins both helpers under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision

  - low-level package-internal token-list iteration helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@tfor` now narrow-iterates grouped token lists item-by-item instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal list rebuild helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@cons` now narrow-appends `\@elt`-style list entries in global scope, `\@removeelement` now narrow-removes exact items from top-level comma-separated token lists instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins both paths under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal argument expansion helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@thirdofthree` now narrow-selects the third argument, `\@expandtwoargs` now narrow-fully-expands two arguments before reinjecting them into the target macro, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins both paths under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - preamble boolean-definition helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local toolchain path: `\newif` now narrow-defines `\iffoo`, `\footrue`, and `\foofalse` style booleans on top of builtin `\iftrue/\iffalse`, skipped-branch scanning now recognizes user-defined boolean conditionals instead of only hard-coded `\ifx/\ifnum/\ifdefined`, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins wrapper class/package boolean option state under a later option-only revision
  - low-level aux-write boolean helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same local toolchain path: `\makeatletter`-scoped `\@fileswtrue`, `\@fileswfalse`, and `\if@filesw` now narrow-toggle and read the common aux-write boolean instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, plain `\nofiles` now narrow-disables that same snapshot-aware state, old snapshots default the state to enabled for compatibility, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins the path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal membership helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\in@` now narrow-checks whether a token-list needle occurs in a token-list haystack, `\ifin@` now reads that snapshot-aware boolean state instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins both helpers under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal hook helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\g@addto@macro` now narrow-appends token lists to an existing macro body in global scope instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins both grouped append and later option-only revision paths under a wrapper class/package stack
  - low-level package-internal token cleanup helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\zap@space` now narrow-strips only space tokens from a token list until builtin `\@empty` instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal empty-argument guards are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@ifempty` now narrow-chooses between empty and nonempty token-list branches instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal nonempty-argument guards are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@ifnotempty` now narrow-chooses between nonempty and empty token-list branches instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - those low-level sanitize/no-op and empty-argument helpers are now also exercised together in one wrapper class/package corpus fixture, so `\@onlypreamble`, `\@onelevel@sanitize`, `\@bsphack`, `\@esphack`, `\zap@space`, `\@ifempty`, `\@ifnotempty`, `\@ifmtarg`, and `\@ifnotmtarg` are no longer only pinned in isolated micro-fixtures
  - low-level kernel branch aliases are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\kernel@ifnextchar` and `\kernel@ifstar` now narrow-delegate to the same optional-argument and star-form branch logic as `\@ifnextchar` / `\@ifstar` instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal temp-switch helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@tempswatrue`, `\@tempswafalse`, and `\if@tempswa` now narrow-toggle and read the common boolean temp switch instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, the switch is preserved in VM snapshot state, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package/class/file version macros are now also fixed and covered at the same provided-date path: `\ProvidesPackage`, `\ProvidesClass`, and `\ProvidesFile` now also define `\ver@...` macros alongside the tracked provided-date maps, so package internals can reuse the same version payload through `\@nameuse{ver@...}` without falling through as undefined control sequences, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal list iteration is now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@for` now narrow-iterates top-level comma-separated lists while preserving grouped list items, and a dedicated corpus fixture pins that path under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level package-internal loop helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@whilenum` now narrow-reinjects numeric-relation loops with `\do{...}` bodies, `\@whilesw` now narrow-reinjects boolean-switch loops terminated by `\fi`, plain `\loop...\repeat` now narrow-collects its body through the top-level `\repeat` delimiter and reinjects it through an internal iterate macro that follows the usual trailing `\if...\else...\fi` control flow, and dedicated corpus fixtures pin all three helpers under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - low-level whitespace-trim helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition path: `\ignorespaces` now narrow-discards only the immediately following run of space tokens instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins both direct use and macro-body use under a later option-only revision
  - low-level job-name helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition path: `\jobname` now narrow-materializes the top-level entry source stem instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, falls back to `texput` when no entry source exists, stays anchored to the toplevel even inside nested `\input` files and `\edef` captures, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level current-module helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition path: `\makeatletter`-scoped `\@currname`, `\@currext`, and `\@currpath` now narrow-materialize the current active source frame's stem, extension, and parent path instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, they stay stable under `\edef` capture and shift correctly when execution moves into nested inputs, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin that path under later option-only revisions
  - low-level filename parsing helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same preamble-definition path: `\filename@parse` now narrow-splits a path token list into `\filename@area`, `\filename@base`, and `\filename@ext` instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, the parsed fields stay usable under `\edef` capture, and a dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixture pins that path under a later option-only revision
  - low-level aux-write helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\newwrite` now narrow-defines distinct stream aliases instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, plain `\openout`/`\closeout` now narrow-consume stream and filename tokens non-visibly, plain `\write` now narrow-consumes stream/body arguments and fully expands the write payload non-visibly, `\immediate` now narrow-behaves as a no-op prefix in front of that path, `\protected@write` continues to narrow-consume stream/prefix/body arguments on the same full-expansion helper, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin those paths with `ABSENT` expectations under later option-only revisions
  - low-level aux-read helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same file-stream path: `\newread` now narrow-defines distinct read-stream aliases instead of falling through as an undefined control sequence, plain `\openin`/`\closein` now narrow-consume stream and filename tokens non-visibly, narrow `\ifeof` now tracks unopened/missing/open/closed stream state through snapshot/restore instead of falling through as an undefined conditional, plain `\read ... to ...` and plain `\readline ... to ...` now narrow-materialize the next config line into a control sequence and fall back to `\relax` at EOF instead of falling through as undefined primitives, and dedicated wrapper class/package corpus fixtures pin those paths under later option-only revisions
  - low-level package-internal identity/sentinel helpers are now also fixed and covered at the same `\makeatletter` path: `\@firstofone` and `\@iden` now narrow-pass through a single argument, builtin `\@empty` and `\@nil` are now defined from VM boot so `\ifx`-style sentinel compares no longer fall through as undefined control sequences, and dedicated corpus fixtures pin those paths under a wrapper class/package stack with a later option-only revision
  - package/class version-guard helpers are now also fixed and covered at the narrow provided-date level: `\IfPackageAtLeastTF` and `\IfClassAtLeastTF` now consult the dates recorded by `\ProvidesPackage`/`\ProvidesClass` instead of falling through as undefined control sequences, `\makeatletter`-scoped `\@ifpackagelater` / `\@ifclasslater` now narrow-match the same provided dates with strict later-than comparison, and dedicated corpus fixtures pin both the high-level and low-level provided-date paths under wrapper class/package stacks with later option-only revisions
  - `xelatex` file-name font lookup is now fixed and covered at the narrow local-font level: the same `\IfFileExists` path now lets a minimal local `fontspec.sty` resolve bare font filenames such as `Example Font.otf`
  - README's first known-issue fixture list is now fully represented by real regressions and a small on-disk `fixtures/arxiv-smoke/*` corpus gate (`crates/latexd/tests/arxiv_smoke.rs`)
  - that corpus gate now checks positive expectations, optional negative expectations (`ABSENT.txt`), optional executed-source expectations (`EXECUTED-EXPECT.txt`), optional revision-artifact expectations (`ARTIFACT-EXPECT.txt`), optional structured JSON expectations (`JSON-EXPECT.txt`), optional revision deletes (`REVN-DELETE.txt`), and optional expected compile failures (`REVN-FAIL.txt`) so raw semantic/package commands cannot quietly leak into output or executed sources, expected rewrites can be asserted directly, concrete artifacts like `semantic.aux` and `build-meta.json` are exercised directly, missing-file and missing package/class failure paths can be covered without a separate harness, and the same fixture can keep going into a later recovery revision after a failed one
  - the same gate now supports optional `revN/` overlays plus `REVN-*` expectation files, so selected fixtures can exercise real multi-revision behavior such as semantic aux backdating, semantic-change rebuilds, and reused-page metadata instead of only first-build success; the current semantic-aux-heavy fixture and the `revtex`-style semantic stack fixture both pin second-revision backdating and third-revision semantic-change rebuild metadata through structured JSON expectations
  - asset-style hardening fixtures now also use the same revision path: `minted-cache` now covers local cache-asset loss and later recovery for `_minted-main/code.pygtex`, while `xelatex-font-filename` pins `font-missing` after deleting the local font asset and `font-found` again after recovery
  - the corpus now also includes bibliography-artifact fixtures that keep visible output stable while changing `\bibliographystyle{...}` or `\bibliography{...}` input order across revisions, so `semantic.aux`/`build-meta.json` must reflect `\bibstyle` and `\bibdata` changes even when page text does not
  - bibliography input loss/recovery is now also pinned as a corpus behavior: deleting `refs.bbl` does not currently hard-fail the semantic path, but it does degrade output to unresolved citation text plus an empty bibliography, and the following recovery revision restores the materialized bibliography text
  - heading-only bibliography semantics are now also in the corpus: a `\printbibheading[heading=bibintoc,title=...]` fixture with no `.bbl` inputs pins `semantic.aux` TOC writes, raw-command stripping, and revision-to-revision title changes through the same multi-revision harness
  - that heading-only bibliography path is now also pinned under a wrapper class/package option stack, so `\printbibheading` title changes and later `twocolumn/unicode -> onecolumn/plain` option changes are exercised together with concrete `semantic.aux` TOC writes instead of only in a standalone article fixture
  - theorem declaration semantics are now also in the corpus: a dedicated fixture changes `\newtheorem` counter scope across revisions and pins the resulting visible numbering, executed-source rewrite, and semantic label artifacts through the same multi-revision harness
  - that theorem declaration path is now also pinned under a wrapper class/package option stack, so `\newtheorem{theorem}{Theorem}[section]` style scope changes are exercised with option forwarding markers still present in visible output and with the same semantic label artifact expectations
  - equation/reference semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps equation labels flowing through `\eqref`, `\autoref`, `\cref`, `\namecref`, `\vref`, and `\crefrange` across a semantic label-set revision and a later option-only revision, so equation-specific reference wording is exercised outside the standalone smokes too
  - float/reference semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps figure/table/algorithm labels flowing through `\autoref`, `\cref`, `\namecref`, and `\vref` across a float-kind revision and a later option-only revision, so float-kind wording is exercised outside the standalone smokes too
  - page-range reference semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps `\pagerefrange`, `\vpagerefrange`, `\vrefrange`, and `\cpagerefrange` flowing through a label-numbering revision and a later option-only revision, so page-range wording is exercised outside the standalone smokes too
  - label-only reference semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps `\labelcref` and `\labelcpageref` flowing through an equation-number revision and a later option-only revision, so cleveref label-only wording is exercised outside the standalone smokes too
  - larger multi-file preamble realism is now also pinned in the corpus: the dedicated `split-preamble-semantic-stack` fixture now uses a wrapper `wrapper.cls -> profile.cls -> article.cls` class chain, a local `shim.sty -> shim.cfg -> shim.def` package/config chain, and a nested `\input{preamble/setup}` -> `\input{preamble/core}` -> `\input{preamble/macros}` / `\input{preamble/theorems}` split so local packages (`hyperxmp`, `cleveref`), theorem declaration rewrite, bibliography materialization, and TOC rewrite all stay active while later revisions exercise a semantic change inside the nested preamble, a later option-only revision, nested preamble-file deletion/recovery, local package deletion/recovery, local class deletion/recovery, and body include deletion/recovery
  - float caption/list semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: one fixture keeps `\caption[Short]{Long}` + `\listoffigures` stable across a caption-title revision and a later option-only revision, while a second fixture does the same for `\captionof{figure}`, so `lof` writes and figure-label title resolution are exercised outside the standalone semantic-aux-heavy paper too
  - short-title TOC semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps `\section[Short]{Long}` consistent across a title-change revision and a later option-only revision, so `semantic.aux` `\contentsline` writes, body long-title materialization, and `\nameref` title resolution are exercised outside the standalone semantic-aux-heavy paper too
  - split-document include filtering is now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture changes `\includeonly{chapters/...}` across revisions, so TOC entries, visible output, executed include files, and semantic labels all follow the selected include set, while a later option-only revision proves the same semantic state can be backdated instead of rebuilt from scratch
  - manual TOC entry semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture changes `\phantomsection` / `\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{...}` titles across revisions, so unnumbered TOC writes, raw-command stripping, and visible TOC/body output are exercised under richer option forwarding too
  - appendix/reference semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: one dedicated fixture keeps `\appendix` lettering, appendix TOC output, `\autoref`, and `\nameref` stable across a title-change revision and a later option-only revision, a second does the same for the `\appendices` synonym, and a third covers book-style chapter appendix/autoref output under a wrapper class stack, so appendix-aware semantic rewrites are exercised outside the standalone article/book smokes too
  - theorem declaration semantics are now also pinned one step deeper under the same wrapper class/package option stack: beyond the plain `\newtheorem` counter-scope fixture, a dedicated theoremstyle/custom-theorem fixture now keeps `\theoremstyle`, `\newtheoremstyle`, and `\swapnumbers` stripped while a section-scoped custom theorem plus shared-counter corollary rewrite survive a semantic title change and a later option-only revision
  - theorem multi-ref semantics are now also pinned under the same wrapper class/package option stack: a dedicated fixture keeps repeated theorem labels flowing through `\cref`, `\namecrefs`, and `\nameref` pluralization/title resolution while option forwarding stays active, so theorem reference surface is no longer only covered by standalone smokes
  - package/class option propagation is now pinned in the corpus: dedicated fixtures now cover `\PassOptionsToPackage{draft|final}{shim}`, `\PassOptionsToClass{twocolumn|onecolumn}{article}`, `\documentclass[...]{wrapper}` forwarding through `\LoadClassWithOptions`, `\DeclareOption*{\PassOptionsToPackage{\CurrentOption}{...}}` and `\DeclareOption*{\PassOptionsToClass{\CurrentOption}{...}}` forwarding to nested package/class wrappers, `\DeclareOption{foo}{\PassOptionsToPackage{\CurrentOption}{...}}` declared-option bodies, `\ExecuteOptions{draft}` default-option behavior for both package and class wrappers with later explicit override, and the common `\ProcessOptions*` variant, so local option chains are checked through visible revision markers
